  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">SAN DIEGO, March 24, 2022 (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- Erasca, Inc.   <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#x201c;Erasca capped off a productive year by achieving all </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">of our </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">2021 clinical and corporate milestones on or ahead of schedule,&#x201d; said Jonathan E. cetuximab </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">in patients with BRAF V600E-mutant ongoing HERKULES-3 trial</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">, and we are excited about   <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Dr. Lim continued, &#x201c;Our CNS-penetrant product candidates continued to advance well in 2021. First, in June 2021, we nominated ERAS-3490, a highly CNS-penetrant KRAS G12C inhibitor and our first homegrown development candidate. This molecule was specifically designed to cross the blood-brain barrier to address the propensity of non-small cell lung cancer to metastasize to the brain, and we are currently on track for an IND filing in the second half of 2022. Second, we were pleased to receive IND clearance of ERAS-801 for the treatment of patients with recurrent glioblastoma multiforme a quarter earlier than expected, and we dosed the first patient in THUNDERBBOLT-1 last month.</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> ERAS-801</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> is</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> an oral EGFR inhibitor with </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">four </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">times higher CNS penetration than approved EGFR inhibitors and the differentiated ability to </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">target </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">both oncogenic EGFR vIII mutations</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> and </font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">wildtype alterations. Overall, our solid cash position, industry leading portfolio</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">,</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> and focused approach </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">will enable us to continue to execute well in 2</font><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">022.&#x201d;</font></p>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(255,255,255,1);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Fourth Quarter and Full Year 2021 Financial Results</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Cash Position: </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Cash, cash equivalents, and investments were $459.2 million as of December 31, 2021, compared to $118.7 million as of December 31, 2020. During 2021, Erasca completed an IPO raising net proceeds of $317.0 million, after deducting underwriting discounts, commissions, and other offering expenses. Erasca expects its current cash, cash equivalents, and investments balance to fund operations into 2024.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Research and Development (R&amp;D) Expenses: </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">R&amp;D expenses were $24.1 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2021, compared to $10.1 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2020. The increase was primarily driven by expenses incurred in connection with clinical trials and preclinical studies, personnel costs due to increased headcount to support increased development activities, and outsourced services and consulting fees. Erasca also recorded $0 and $54.0 million of in-process research and development expense during the quarters ended December 31, 2021 and 2020 for upfront and milestone payments and stock issuances under certain of our acquisition and license agreements. R&amp;D expenses were $73.9 million for the full year ended December 31, 2021, compared to $29.6 million for the full year ended December 31, 2020.  Erasca also recorded $10.8 million and $71.7 million of in-process research and development expense during the full years ended December 31, 2021 and 2020, respectively, for upfront and milestone payments and stock issuances under certain of our acquisition and license agreements.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">General and Administrative (G&amp;A) Expenses: </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">G&amp;A expenses were $6.9 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2021, compared to $2.9 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2020. The increase was primarily driven by personnel costs, insurance costs, and facilities and related costs. G&amp;A expenses were $22.6 million for the full year ended December 31, 2021, compared to $8.0 million for the full year ended December 31, 2020. For the full year ended December 31, 2021, $17.5 million was recorded as additional G&amp;A expense for the common shares issued to the Erasca Foundation in conjunction with Erasca&#x2019;s IPO.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Net Loss:</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> Net loss was $30.5 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2021, compared to $61.9 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2020.  For the full year ended December 31, 2021, Erasca reported a net loss of $122.8 million, inclusive of the $17.5 million in expense recorded for the common shares issued to the Erasca Foundation, or $(1.85) per basic and diluted share, compared to a net loss of $101.7 million, or $(4.83) per basic and diluted share, for the full year ended December 31, 2020.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">About Erasca</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"><br>At Erasca, our name is our mission: To </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">eras</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">e </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">ca</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">ncer. We are a clinical-stage precision oncology company singularly focused on discovering, developing, and commercializing therapies for patients with RAS/MAPK pathway-driven cancers. Our company was co-founded by leading pioneers in precision oncology and RAS targeting to create novel therapies and combination regimens designed to comprehensively shut down the RAS/MAPK pathway for the treatment of cancer. We have assembled what we believe to be the deepest RAS/MAPK pathway-focused pipeline in the industry. We believe our team&#x2019;s capabilities and experience, further guided by our scientific advisory board which includes the world&#x2019;s leading experts in the RAS/MAPK pathway, uniquely position us to achieve our bold mission of</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">

Actual results may differ from those set forth in this press release due to the risks and uncertainties inherent in our business, including, without limitation: our approach to the discovery and development of product candidates based on our singular focus on shutting down the RAS/MAPK pathway, a novel and unproven approach; regulatory developments in the United States and foreign countries; our dependence on third parties for our existing collaboration and supply agreements and we may not realize any benefits from such agreements; our ability to obtain and maintain intellectual property protection for our product candidates and maintain our rights under intellectual property licenses; our ability to fund our operating plans with our current cash, cash equivalents, and investments; in our quarterly report on Form 10-Q for the three months ended June 30, 2021, and any subsequent filings with the SEC.
